0.0;\n\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_registers; ++i) {\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = 0;\n\n    if (overflow_bucket_.find(i) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    }\n\n    // Reconstruct the full position value\n    uint64_t position = (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) | dense_val;\n\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(position));\n  }\n\n  // E = CONSTANT * m^2 / sum, where m = 2^n_leading_bits\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_registers);\n  double uint64_t position = (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) | dense_val;\n\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(position));\n  }\n\n  // E = CONSTANT * m^2 / sum, where m = 2^n_leading_bits\n // Extract register index from the first n_leading_bits\n  uint64_t register_idx = hash & ((1ULL << n_leading_bits_) - 1);\n\n  // Get the remaining bits\n  hash_t w = hash >> n_leading_bits_;\n\n  //  // Update if new position is larger\n    if (position > current_position) {\n      dense_bucket_[register_idx] = dense_val;\n      if (overflow_val > 0) {\n        overflow_bucket_[register_idx] = dense_val;\n\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(position));\n  }\n\n  // E = CONSTANT * m^2 / sum, where m = 2^n_leading_bits\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_registers);\n  double
